\begin{entry}
\word{dhAraNayoVga}
\meaning{\arthanonum{(noVDi. dhAraNa).}
\ullekha{anavaciCxnanx teYladhAreyaMte shivadhAyxnamaM mADutiralu A dhAyxnAkAradiM karigoMDa vasutxvinoLu A manavu nishacxlamAgaladeV dhAraNayoVga noVDA (aKaMDeV. 220-61); dhAyxnisidalilx AyA liMgagaLu AyA cakarxgaLalilx sAthxpayxvAguvuvu. idariMda BAva, karaNa, mana muKayxvAda savARMgadalilx A liMgavu toLagi beLagahatatxlu A liMgadoDane AcaraNegaLuMTAguvuvu. ideV dhAraNayoVgavu (shivAkoV. 48-44); yama, niyama, Asana, pArxNAyAma, parxtAyxhAra... savARMgadalilx dharisuvudiVga dhAraNayoVga... (savasaM. 11; toVMTasi. 364-170); AcAraliMgava aMgeYyoLagaLavaDisi... jAgarxtf savxpanxdalilx pUjisuva dhAraNayoVgadoLiduR... (savasaM. 11; GanaliM. 727-338); inunx dhAraNayoVgada lakaSxNaveMtene... (savasaM. 14; SaNumxKa. 737-332); haThayoVga laMbikAyoVga AtamxyoVga... ipupxdu dhAraNayoVga... (savasaM. 6; Adayayx. 1141-357); manava sakaleVMdirxyaMgaLa keVrigaLalilx... sUsaliVyade dharisikoMDihudeV dhAraNayovga noVDA... (savasaM. 13; bAlasaM. 359-164).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{dhAraNasidadhx}
\meaning{\arthanonum{aSATxMgayoVga sAdhanegaLanunx mADida eMTu parxkArada sAdhakaralilx obabx; tananx citatxvanunx parabarxhamxnalilx nelegoLisidavanu.}
\ullekha{tAM shuBAsharxyadalilx tacicxtatxvu meVNadaMtagaRtamumAda dhAraNasidadhxru ...tamamx nija susavxrUpaM naviVna paramAtamxnoLageVkarasavAgi beLasutetx (viVsheYpu. 5-80-21).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{dhAraNA}
\meaning{\artha{yama, niyama, Asana, pArxNAyAma, parxtAyxhAra, dhAyxna,
dhAraNa, samAdhi eMba aSATxMgayoVgagaLalilx oMdu. paramAtamxnalilx manasasxnunx daqDhavAgi

avayavagaLalilx athavA shuBavAda horagina vasutxvinalilx citatxvanunx sithxravAgi
nililxsuva aBAyxsa.}}

\begin{entry}

  AMtarika vidhAna. 4. seVvana (pAdaseVve) Bakitx : ililx vAsatxvavAgi
sAdhakanu sAkaSuTx AdhAyxtimxka parxgati sAdhisiruvavara pAdaseVve,

vaMdane. 7. dAsayx : yAvudeV kAyaRdalilx tAnu mADideneMba ahaMkAra

mADuvudelalxvU shivanigAgi mAtarx eMdU tiLiyutAtxne. 8. saKayx :
senxVhitanAdavanu yAvAgalU tananx pirxya geLeyana joteyalilxralu
bayasutAtxnoV, hAgeyeV nijavAda Bakatxnu yAvAgalU parashivana
saMgadalilx bayasutAtxne. nijavAda saKayx lABada kaDe gamana

\begin{entry}
\word{niHshabadxbarxhamx ucayxteV}
\meaning{\artha{``niHshabadxveV barxhamx eMdu heVLalAgutatxde''. barxhamx
  (parashiva)nanunx tananx savxMta anuBAvada mUlaka aritavanu
  parashivana bagege EnanUnx heVLuvudilalx. adakekx kAraNaviSeTxV: nAvu
parxtiyoMdu shabadxvanUnx iMdirxyAnuBavada mUlakaveV
tiLidukoLuLxtetxVve. iMdirxyAnuBavada mUlaka bArada BASe ilalxveV
ilalx. AdudariMda nAvu yAvudeV riVtiya BASeyanunx upayoVgisidarU adu
parxtayxkaSxvAgi athavA paroVkaSxvAgi iMdirxyAnuBavada vasutxgaLige
anavxyisutatxde. Adare parabarxhamx nAvu noVDida, nAvu muTiTxda, nAvu
rucisida, nAvu keVLida, yAva vasutxvinaMteyU ilalxvAdudariMda,
avananunx namage gotitxruva yAva shabadxgaLiMdalU vaNiRsalu
sAdhayxvilalx. Aga barxhamxnanunx tiLidavaru avanunx vaNiRsa hoVgi
mUka (niHshabadx) rAgutAtxre}}
\meaning{\artha{eraDaneyadAgi, nAvu yAvudeV vasutxvanunx iMdirxyAnuBavada mUlaka
  tiLidukoLuLxvAga jAcnxtaq jecnxVyagaLa devxYtavanunx
  anusarisutetxVve. Adare parashivananunx aritavaru I devxYtakekx
  horagAdudariMda avaru parashivananunx oMdu jecnxVyadaMte
  vaNiRsalAraru. AgalU avaru niHshabadx.}}
\end{entry}

\ullekha{apipxdaDe suKavilalx melidaDe ruciyilalx kUDalasaMgamadeVvA nijavilalxdavana Bakitx (savasaM. 1; basava. 126-34); haqdayapiVThava balidu sadamalada beLaginiM Palapadavanodedu nijadali niMdenu (padagoV. {\rm{ii}}-4); nimaRlavAda nijavana{\ri}yaru vamaRvilalxde vamaR hoMdisi nuDivaru (kaDasavx. 2-40-1).}}

\ullekha{mAkaRMDeVyamahAmuni sevxVcACxmaraNi enisikoMDanalalxde liMgada 
nijavana{\ri}yanu (savasaM. 1; basava. 858-224); shivana nija tiLivude mahAjAcnxna (kaDasavx. 3-58-2).}}

\ullekha{shiva, paravasutx, nija ...paramAtamx I shabadxgaLelalxvU paramAtamx athavA deVvara doyxVtakavAgive (shivAkoV. 12-18); manavaMcaneye anayxliMgAcaRne... adu nijavalalx nijavalalx... \begin{entry}

  managaMDidadxrU, anuBAvada mUlaka neVravAgi aritukoMDAgaleV

kANe'', (9:92) eMbalilx nishacxyada, badalu ``nishacxla''vanunx

\begin{entry}
\word{nUroMdu sathxla (EkoVtatxra shatasathxla)}
\src{va}
\mng{vacanagaLalilx alalxlilx nUroMdu sathxla athavA EkoVtatxra
  shatasathxla eMba pada parxyoVgavAgidadxrU, A nUroMdu
  sathxlagaLAvuvu, avugaLa vishiSaTx lakaSxNagaLAvuvu eMbudara vivara
  sikukxvudilalx. I vivaragaLige nAvu, idanunx vivaravAgi tiLisiruva
  sidAdhxMtashiKAmaNiyanunx avalaMbisabeVkAgutatxde. jakakxNAyaRru
  racisida `EkoVtatxra shatasathxla'vU ililx upayoVgakaravAgidadxrU,
  avaru yAvobabx sharaNara nUroMdu sathxla parikalapxneyanUnx kuritu
  heVLuvudilalx. sidAdhxMta shiKAmaNiya sidAdhxMtakekx hoVluvaMtha
  vacanagaLanunx Ayudx avugaLanunx nUroMdu sathxlagaLaDiyalilx
  taMdidAdxre.}\\
\imng{nUroMdu sathxlagaLanunx muKayxvAgi, aMga SaTfsathxla matutx
  liMga SaTfsathxla eMdu eraDu BAga mADalAgide. modalaneyadu
  nalavatAnxlukx sathxlagaLanonxLagoMDare, eraDaneyadu aivatetxVLu
  sathxlagaLanonxLagoLuLxtatxde.}\\
\imng{vacanakArarelalxrU SaTfsathxla sidAdhxMtada
  parxtipAdakarAgidadxrU, A sidAdhxM\-takUkx nUroMdu sathxla
  sidAdhxMtakUkx viroVdha athavA vayxtAyxsa baradaMte, averaDanUnx
  samanavxyagoLisidAdxre. aMdare, nUroMdu sathxlagaLanunx I
  keLaginaMte haMcidAdxre:}\\
\imng{(a) aMga SaTfsathxlagaLaDiyalilx I keLagina 44 sathxlagaLu
  barutatxve:}\\
\imng{1. BakatxsathxladaDiyalilx 15 sathxlagaLu (avu yAvuveMdare :
  piMDasathxla, piMDajAcnxnasathxla; saMsAra heVyasathxla,
  gurukaruNasathxla, liMgadhAraNasathxla, viBUtisathxla, rudArxkiSxsathxla, paMcAkaSxrisathxla, Bakitxsathxla, (athavA
  BakitxmAgaRkirxyAsathxla), uBayasathxla, tirxvidha saMpatitxna
  sathxla, catuviRdhasArAyasathxla, upAdhimATasathxla, nirupAdhimATasathxla matutx sahajamATasathxla).}\\
\imng{2. maheVshavxrasathxladaDiyalilx oMbatutx sathxlagaLu (avu
  yAvudeMdare : maheVshavxrasathxla, liMganiSAThxsathxla,
  pUvARsharxyinirasanasathxla, vAgadevxYtanirasanasathxla, AhAvxnanirasanasathxla, aSaTxtanumUtiRnirasanasathxla, savaRgatanirasanasathxla, shiva\-jaganamxyasathxla, BakatxdeVhika
  liMgasathxla).}\\
\imng{3. parxsAdisathxladaDiyalilx ELu sathxlagaLu (aveMdare :
  parxsAdisathxla, gurumahAtamxyXsathxla, liMgamahAtamxyXsathxla,
  sharaNamahAtamxyXsathxla, jaMgamamahAtamxyXsathxla,
  BakatxmahAtamxyXsathxla, parxsAdamahAtamxyXsathxla).}\\
\imng{4. pArxNaliMgisathxlavu aidu
  sathxlagaLanonxLagoLuLxtatxde. (aveMdare : pArxNa\-liMgisathxla,
  pArxNaliMgAcaRnasathxla, shivayoVgasamAdhisathxla,
  liMga\-nijasathxla, aMganiMgasathxla).}\\
\imng{5. sharaNasathxlavu nAlukx
  sathxlagaLanonxLagoLuLxtatxde. (aveMdare : sharaNasathxla,
  tAmasanirasanasathxla, nideRVshanasathxla, shiVlasaMpAdanA
  sathxla).}\\
\imng{6. aikayxsathxlavu nAlukx
  sathxlagaLanonxLagoLuLxtatxde. (aveMdare : aikayxsathxla, savARcArasaMpatitxna sathxla, EkaBAjanasathxla, sahaBAjanasathxla).}\\
\imng{(A) liMgaSaTfsathxladaDiyalilx uLida 57 sathxlagaLu
  barutatxve. avugaLa vivara:}\\
\imng{(1) AcAraliMgasathxladaDiyalilx : diVkASxgurusathxla,
  shikASxgurusathxla, jAcnxnagurusathxla, kirxyAliMgasathxla,
  BAvaliMgasathxla, jAcnxnaliMgasathxla, savxyasathxla, carasathxla
  matutx parasathxla eMba oMbatutx sathxlagaLu barutatxve.}\\
\imng{(2) guruliMgasathxlavu kirxyAgamasathxla, BAvAgamasathxla,
  jAcnxnAgamasathxla, sakAyasathxla, akAyasathxla, parakAyasathxla,
  dhamARcArasathxla, BAvAcArasathxla, jAcnxnAcArasathxla eMba oMbatutx

  oLagoLuLxtatxde. aveMdare : kAyAnugarxhasathxla,
  iMdirxyAnugarxhasathxla, pArxNAnugarxhasathxla, kAyApiRtasathxla,
  karaNApiRtasathxla, BAvApiRtasathxla, shiSayxsathxla,

\begin{entry}
\word{paMcakameVRMdirxya}
\src{saM}
\mng{mUvatAtxru tatAtxvXMtagaRta kirxyAsAdhaka
iMdirxyagaLu. vAkf, pANi, pAda, pAyu (guda), upasathx (jananeVMdirxya)-ivu

\mng{ucAcxraNakirxyege heVtu vAkf (mAtu), koDuva-sivxVkarisuva kirxyege heVtu pANi
(keYgaLu). hoVguva matutx baruva kirxyege heVtu pAda (kAlugaLu), uMDa ananxvu
jiVNaRvAgalu malavisajaRne kirxyege heVtu pAyu (guda), reVtasusx, mUtarxgaLa
tAyxgakirxyege sAdhana upasathx (jananeVMdirxya) eMba paMcakameRVMdirxyagaLu.}
\begin{shl}
jAcnxneVMdirxyANi paMcApi paMcakameRVMdirxyANi ca |
\end{shl}

\begin{shl}
vAkf ca pANishacx pAdashacx pAyushocxVpasathxmitayxpi |\\
kameRVMdirxyANi paMceYSAM guNAH paMcaparxkiVtiRtAH ||
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(shi.ta.ra., 9. 3.12)}
\begin{shl}
tatarx ucAcxraNakirxyAheVtuvARkf, dAnAdAnAdikirxyAheVtuH pANiH, gamanAgamana-
kirxyAsAdhanaM pAdaH, BukatxjiVNaRmalaparitAyxgasAdhanaM pAyuH, reVtoVmUtarx-
paritAyxgakirxyAsAdhanamupasathxkamf |
\end{shl}
\pauthor{(shi.maM., pu. 54)}
\SEE{mUvatAtxru tatatxvX}

\src{kA}
